The F50 duo fibre brush is not dense enough or have enough white fibers to be used as a stippling brush, although I do like it for blush application. The E40 tapered blending brush is very loose and floppy - useless for applying color to the crease or for blending. It also blew out and lost shape after washing. The other brushes are quite good. I purchased the complete brush set because I had bought the 3 piece synthetic brush set earlier and was very impressed by it. I really love the F80, F82, and F84. The large shader brush in my set had weird bristles, as if production of this brush was flawed because the cut for the brush shape at the top wasn't so great.<br /><br />The small angle brush is the one I use the most, for gel eyeliners. Other brushes I enjoyed in this set were the large angled contour and eye shading brush.<br /><br />After a bunch of washings, the large powder brush, eye shading, and large angled contour are the ones that seem to shed the most, but not with each wash. For example, my large angled contour might shed 4-5 strands every 2-3 washes while my large powder brush sheds just 1 strand with each wash.<br /><br />Overall, this set is great for beginners who are looking for an affordable first set. However, I do agree with some other reviews that the quality in the entire set isn't consistent.
